    ZEO = {

      set_temp_variable = { amount_of_ms_var_negative = ROOT.amount_of_ms_var }

#オデッサ
#4000 MS
country_event = {
  id = zeon.4000
  title = zeon.4000.t
  desc = zeon.4000.d
  picture = GFX_country_zeon4000

  is_triggered_only = yes

  option = {
    name = zeon.4000.l
    trigger = {
      has_manpower > 76000
      OR = {
        AND = {
          check_variable = { how_many_drop_earth = 2 }
          has_equipment = {
            archetype_ms05 > 5400
          }
        }
        AND = {
          check_variable = { how_many_drop_earth = 3 }
          has_equipment = {
            archetype_ms05 > 3600
          }
        }
        AND = {
          check_variable = { how_many_drop_earth = 4 }
          has_equipment = {
            archetype_ms05 > 1800
          }
        }
      }
      has_equipment = {
        archetype_ms_weapon_heathawk > 1800
      }
      has_equipment = {
        archetype_ms_weapon_machinegun > 1800
      }
      has_equipment = {
        archetype_ms_shield > 1800
      }
      has_equipment = {
        infantry_equipment > 500
      }
      has_equipment = {
        support_equipment > 2750
      }
    }
    add_manpower = -76000
    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
      type = archetype_ms05
      amount = -1800
    }
    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
      type = archetype_ms_weapon_heathawk
      amount = -1800
    }
    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
      type = archetype_ms_weapon_machinegun
      amount = -1800
    }
    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
      type = archetype_ms_shield
      amount = -1800
    }
    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
      type = infantry_equipment
      amount = -500
    }
    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
      type = support_equipment
      amount = -2750
    }
    load_oob = "ZEO_drop_odessa_ms_50"
    country_event = { id = zeon.40001 days = 7 }
    country_event = { id = zeon.4001 }
    ai_chance = {
      base = 0
    }
  }
  option = {
    name = zeon.4000.k
    trigger = {
      has_manpower > 68400
      OR = {
        AND = {
          check_variable = { how_many_drop_earth = 2 }
          has_equipment = {
            archetype_ms05 < 5400
          }
          has_equipment = {
            archetype_ms05 > 4860
          }
        }
        AND = {
          check_variable = { how_many_drop_earth = 3 }
          has_equipment = {
            archetype_ms05 < 3600
          }
          has_equipment = {
            archetype_ms05 > 3240
          }
        }
        AND = {
          check_variable = { how_many_drop_earth = 4 }
          has_equipment = {
            archetype_ms05 < 1800
          }
          has_equipment = {
            archetype_ms05 > 1620
          }
        }
      }
      has_equipment = {
        archetype_ms_weapon_heathawk > 1620
      }
      has_equipment = {
        archetype_ms_weapon_machinegun > 1620
      }
      has_equipment = {
        archetype_ms_shield > 1620
      }
      has_equipment = {
        infantry_equipment > 450
      }
      has_equipment = {
        support_equipment > 2475
      }
    }
    add_manpower = -68400
    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
      type = archetype_ms05
      amount = -1620
    }
    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
      type = archetype_ms_weapon_heathawk
      amount = -1620
    }
    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
      type = archetype_ms_weapon_machinegun
      amount = -1620
    }
    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
      type = archetype_ms_shield
      amount = -1620

country_event = {
  id = zeon.4020

  desc = zeon.4020.d
  picture = GFX_country_zeon4000

  is_triggered_only = yes

  option = {
    name = zeon.4020.l
    trigger = {
      has_manpower > 76000
      OR = {
        AND = {
          check_variable = { how_many_drop_earth = 2 }
          has_equipment = {
            archetype_ms05 > 5400
          }
        }
        AND = {
          check_variable = { how_many_drop_earth = 3 }
          has_equipment = {
            archetype_ms05 > 3600
          }
        }
